-- Creating schema and table for ticket_sales_physical
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE ticket_sales_physical (
  sale_id INT,
  ticket_price FLOAT,
  payment_method STRING,
  ticket_id INT,
  purchase_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  visit_hour INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  customer_id INT,
  visit_date DATE,
  purchase_channel STRING,
  purchase_date DATE,
  discount_percent INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN
);

-- Creating schema and table for ticket_sales_online
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE ticket_sales_online (
  sale_id INT,
  ticket_price FLOAT,
  payment_method STRING,
  ticket_id INT,
  purchase_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  visit_hour INT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  customer_id INT,
  visit_date DATE,
  purchase_channel STRING,
  purchase_date DATE,
  discount_percent INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN
);

-- Creating schema and table for merchandise_sales_physical
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE merchandise_sales_physical (
  ticket_id INT,
  quantity INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  customer_id INT,
  category STRING,
  staff_member STRING,
  payment_method STRING,
  is_weekend BOOLEAN,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  days_to_halloween INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN,
  sale_id INT,
  total_price FLOAT,
  unit_price FLOAT,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  sale_date DATE,
  sale_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  product_name STRING,
  product_id INT,
  discount_applied INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for merchandise_sales_online
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS sales;
USE SCHEMA sales;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE merchandise_sales_online (
  ticket_id INT,
  quantity INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  customer_id INT,
  category STRING,
  staff_member FLOAT,
  payment_method STRING,
  is_weekend BOOLEAN,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  days_to_halloween INT,
  is_online_sale BOOLEAN,
  sale_id INT,
  total_price FLOAT,
  unit_price FLOAT,
  haunted_house_id INT,
  sale_date DATE,
  sale_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
  product_name STRING,
  product_id INT,
  discount_applied INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for maintenance_costs
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS park_internal;
USE SCHEMA park_internal;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE maintenance_costs (
  haunted_house_id INT,
  date TIMESTAMP,
  maintenance_type STRING,
  prop_repairs FLOAT,
  maintenance_cost FLOAT,
  equipment_maintenance FLOAT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  structural_repairs FLOAT,
  cost_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for supplies_costs

  haunted_house_id INT,
  supplier STRING,
  makeup_supplies FLOAT,
  cleaning_supplies FLOAT,
  date TIMESTAMP,
  prop_supplies FLOAT,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  supplies_cost FLOAT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  costume_supplies FLOAT,
  cost_id INT
);

-- Creating schema and table for haunted_houses
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS park_assets;
USE SCHEMA park_assets;
CREATE OR REPLACE TABLE haunted_houses (
  theme STRING,
  accessibility_friendly STRING,
  min_age_requirement INT,
  house_status STRING,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP,
  opening_year INT,
  house_size_sqft INT,
  park_area STRING,
  house_name STRING,
  duration_minutes INT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP,
  max_capacity_per_group INT,
  fear_level INT,
  haunted_house_id INT
);
